<h1 _ngcontent-lxd-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="ArkTS语言介绍"> ArkTS语言介绍 </h1>

<div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>ArkTS是一种设计用于构建高性能应用的编程语言。它在继承TypeScript语法的基础上进行了优化，以提供更高的性能和开发效率。</p>    <p>许多编程语言在设计之初未考虑移动设备，导致应用运行缓慢、低效且功耗大。随着移动设备在日常生活中越来越普遍，针对移动环境的编程语言优化需求日益增加。ArkTS专为解决这些问题而设计，聚焦提高运行效率。</p>    <p>TypeScript是在JavaScript基础上通过添加类型定义扩展而来的，ArkTS则是TypeScript的进一步扩展。TypeScript提供了一种更结构化的JavaScript编码方法，深受开发者喜爱。ArkTS保持了TypeScript的大部分语法，旨在为现有的TypeScript开发者提供高度兼容的体验，帮助移动开发者快速上手。</p>    <p>ArkTS的一大特性是它专注于低运行时开销。ArkTS对TypeScript的动态类型特性施加了更严格的限制，以减少运行时开销，提高执行效率。通过取消动态类型特性，ArkTS代码能更有效地被运行前编译和优化，从而实现更快的应用启动和更低的功耗。</p>    <p>ArkTS语言设计中考虑了与TypeScript和JavaScript的互通性。许多移动应用开发者希望重用TypeScript和JavaScript代码及库，因此ArkTS提供与TypeScript和JavaScript的无缝互通，使开发者可以轻松集成TypeScript和JavaScript代码到应用中，充分利用现有代码和库进行ArkTS开发。</p>    <p>本教程将指导开发者了解ArkTS的核心功能、语法和最佳实践，助力开发者使用ArkTS高效构建高性能的移动应用。</p>    <p>如需详细了解ArkTS语言，请参阅<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-overview">ArkTS具体指南</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-tools-overview" target="_blank">DevEco Studio</a>。</p>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 80px;">     <h2 id="基本知识">基本知识<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="基本知识" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 853px;">     <h3 id="声明" class="firsth2">声明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="声明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>ArkTS通过声明引入变量、常量、类型和函数。</p>     <p><strong>变量声明</strong></p>     <p>使用关键字let声明的变量可以在程序执行期间具有不同的值。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">hi</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>;</li><li>hi = <span class="hljs-string">'hello, world'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>常量声明</strong></p>     <p>使用关键字const声明的常量为只读类型，只能被赋值一次。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-attr">hello</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>对常量重新赋值会造成编译时错误。</p>     <p><strong>自动类型推断</strong></p>     <p>如果变量或常量的声明包含初始值，开发者无需显式指定类型，因为ArkTS规范已列举了所有允许自动推断类型的场景。</p>     <p>以下示例中，两条声明语句都是有效的，两个变量都是string类型：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">hi1</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> hi2 = <span class="hljs-string">'hello, world'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 5569px;">     <h3 id="类型">类型<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="类型" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>基本类型和引用类型</strong></p>     <p>基本数据类型包括number、string等简单类型，它们可以准确地表示单一的数据类型。对基本类型的存储和访问都是直接的，比较时直接比较其值。</p>     <p>引用类型包括对象、数组和函数等复杂数据结构。这些类型通过引用访问数据，对象和数组可以包含多个值或键值对，函数则可以封装可执行的代码逻辑。引用类型在内存中通过指针访问数据，修改引用会影响原始数据。</p>     <p><strong>number类型</strong></p>     <p>ArkTS提供number类型，任何整数和浮点数都可以被赋给此类型的变量。</p>     <p>数字字面量包括整数字面量和十进制浮点数字面量。</p>     <p>整数字面量包括以下类别：</p>     <ul>      <li>十进制整数，由数字序列组成。例如：0、117、-345。</li>      <li>十六进制整数，以0x（或0X）开头，包含数字（0-9）和字母a-f或A-F。例如：0x1123、0x00111、-0xF1A7。</li>      <li>八进制整数，以0o（或0O）开头，只能包含数字（0-7）。例如：0o777。</li>      <li>二进制整数，以0b（或0B）开头，只能包含数字0和1。例如：0b11、0b0011、-0b11。</li>     </ul>     <p>浮点数字面量包括以下部分：</p>     <ul>      <li>十进制整数，可为有符号数（前缀为“+”或“-”）。</li>      <li>小数点（“.”）。</li>      <li>小数部分（由十进制数字字符串表示）。</li>      <li>指数部分，以“e”或“E”开头，后跟有符号（前缀为“+”或“-”）或无符号整数。</li>     </ul>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> n1 = <span class="hljs-number">3.14</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> n2 = <span class="hljs-number">3.141592</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> n3 = <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> n4 = <span class="hljs-number">1e2</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(<span class="hljs-params">n: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (n &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> n * <span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(n - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(n1)  <span class="hljs-comment">//  7.660344000000002</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(n2)  <span class="hljs-comment">//  7.680640444893748</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(n3)  <span class="hljs-comment">//  1</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">factorial</span>(n4)  <span class="hljs-comment">//  9.33262154439441e+157</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>number类型在表示大整数（即超过-9007199254740991~9007199254740991）时会造成精度丢失。在开发时可以按需使用BigInt类型来确保精度：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" <span class="hljs-title class_">BigInt</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999999'</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-variable function_">toString</span>());</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>boolean类型</strong></p>     <p>boolean类型由true和false两个逻辑值组成。</p>     <p>通常在条件语句中使用boolean类型的变量：</p>     <div </li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (isDone) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Done!'</span>);</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>string类型</strong></p>     <p>string类型代表字符序列，可以使用转义字符来表示字符。</p>     <p>字符串字面量由单引号（'）或双引号（"）之间括起来的零个或多个字符组成。字符串字面量还有一特殊形式，是用反向单引号（`）括起来的模板字面量。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s1 = <span class="hljs-string">'Hello, world!\n'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s2 = <span class="hljs-string">'this is a string'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> a = <span class="hljs-string">'Success'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s3 = <span class="hljs-string">`The result is <span class="hljs-subst">${a}</span>`</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>void类型</strong></p>     <p>void类型用于指定函数没有返回值。</p>     <p>此类型只有一个值，同样是void。由于void是引用类型，因此它可以用于泛型类型参数。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Class</span>&lt;T&gt; {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">//...</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">instance</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Class</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>&gt;;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>Object类型</strong></p>     <p>Object类型是所有引用类型的基类型。任何值，包括基本类型的值，都可以直接被赋给Object类型的变量（基本类型值会被自动装箱）。</p>     <p>object类型用于表示除基本类型外的类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">o1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">o2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span> = [<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>];</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">o3</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span> = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">o4</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">object</span> = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>];</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>array类型</strong></p>     <p>array类型，即数组，是由可赋值给数组声明中指定的元素类型的数据组成的对象。</p>     <p>数组可由数组复合字面量赋值。数组复合字面量是用方括号括起来的零个或多个表达式列表，每个表达式为数组中的一个元素。数组的长度由数组中元素的个数确定。数组中第一个元素的索引为0。</p>     <p>以下示例将创建包含三个元素的数组：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">names</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>[] = [<span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Carol'</span>];</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>enum类型</strong></p>     <p>enum类型，即枚举类型，是预先定义的一组命名值的值类型，其中命名值又称为枚举常量。</p>     <p>使用枚举常量时必须以枚举类型名称为前缀。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">Red</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Green</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Blue</span> }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">c</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Red</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>常量表达式用于显式设置枚举常量的值。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">White</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0xFF</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Grey</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0x7F</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Black</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0x00</span> }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">c</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">ColorSet</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Black</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>Union类型</strong></p>     <p>Union类型，即联合类型，是由多个类型组合成的引用类型。联合类型包含了变量可能的所有类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'frog'</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> | <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span> | <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span> | <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> | <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// Cat、Dog、Frog是一些类型（类或接口）</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">animal</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span>();</li><li>animal = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span>();</li><li>animal = <span class="hljs-number">42</span>;</li><li>animal = <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>;</li><li>animal = <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 可以将类型为联合类型的变量赋值为任何组成类型的有效值</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>可以使用不同机制获取联合类型中的特定类型值。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> { sleep () {}; meow () {} }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span> { sleep () {}; bark () {} }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span> { sleep () {}; leap () {} }</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> | <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span> | <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">animal: Animal</span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (animal <span class="hljs-keyword">instanceof</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Frog</span>) {  <span class="hljs-comment">// 判断animal是否是Frog类型</span></li><li>    animal.<span class="hljs-title function_">leap</span>();  <span class="hljs-comment">// animal在这里是Frog类型</span></li><li>  }</li><li>  animal.<span class="hljs-title function_">sleep</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Animal具有sleep方法</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>Aliases类型</strong></p>     <p>Aliases类型为匿名类型（如数组、函数、对象字面量或联合类型）提供名称，或为已定义的类型提供替代名称。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 二维数组类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Matrix</span> = <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>[][];</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-attr">gameBoard</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Matrix</span> = [</li><li>  [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>],</li><li>  [<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>]</li><li>];</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 函数类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Handler</span> = <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">s: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, no: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-attr">repeatString</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Handler</span> = <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">str, times</span>) =&gt;</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> str.<span class="hljs-title function_">repeat</span>(times);</li><li>};</li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-title function_">repeatString</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'abc'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>)); <span class="hljs-comment">// 'abcabcabc'</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 泛型函数类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Predicate</span>&lt;T&gt; = <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">x: T</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">boolean</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-attr">isEven</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Predicate</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">num</span>) =&gt;</span> num % <span class="hljs-number">2</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 可为空的对象类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">NullableObject</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> {}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">animalData</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">NullableObject</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">emptyData</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">NullableObject</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2960px;">     <h3 id="运算符">运算符<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="运算符" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>赋值运算符</strong></p>     <p>赋值运算符=，使用方式如x=y。</p>     <p>复合赋值运算符将赋值与运算符组合在一起，例如：a += b 等价于 a = a + b，</p>     <p>其中的 += 即为复合赋值运算符</p>     <p>复合赋值运算符包括：+=、-=、*=、/=、%=、&lt;&lt;=、&gt;&gt;=、&gt;&gt;&gt;=、&amp;=、|=、^=。</p>     <p><strong>比较运算符</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">运算符</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">===</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果两个操作数严格相等（对于不同类型的操作数认为是不相等的），则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">!==</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果两个操作数严格不相等（对于不同类型的操作数认为是不相等的），则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">==</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果两个操作数相等，则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">!=</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果两个操作数不相等，则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果左操作数大于右操作数，则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">&gt;=</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果左操作数大于或等于右操作数，则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">&lt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果左操作数小于右操作数，则返回true。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">&lt;=</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">如果左操作数小于或等于右操作数，则返回true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>===与==的区别：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// ==只比较目标的值相等</span></li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">String</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span> == <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>)); <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// ===比较目标的值和类型都相等</span></li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">String</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span> === <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>)); <span class="hljs-comment">// false</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>算术运算符</strong></p>     <p>一元运算符包括：-、+、--、++。</p>     <p>二元运算符列举如下：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.14.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">运算符</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.14.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">+</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">加法</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">减法</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">*</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">乘法</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">/</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">除法</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">%</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">除法后余数</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>位运算符</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.16.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">运算符</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.16.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a &amp; b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">按位与：如果两个操作数的对应位都为1，则将这个位设置为1，否则设置为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a | b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">按位或：如果两个操作数的相应位中至少有一个为1，则将这个位设置为1，否则设置为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a ^ b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">按位异或：如果两个操作数的对应位不同，则将这个位设置为1，否则设置为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">~ a</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">按位非：反转操作数的位。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a &lt;&lt; b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">左移：将a的二进制表示向左移b位。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a &gt;&gt; b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">算术右移：将a的二进制表示向右移b位，带符号扩展。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a &gt;&gt;&gt; b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">逻辑右移：将a的二进制表示向右移b位，左边补0。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>逻辑运算符</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.18.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">运算符</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.18.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a &amp;&amp; b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">逻辑与</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">a || b</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">逻辑或</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">! a</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">逻辑非</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>instanceof运算符</strong></p>     <p>instanceof运算符用于在运行时检查一个对象是否是指定类或其子类的实例。</p>     <p>示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>obj <span class="hljs-keyword">instanceof</span> className</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>返回值类型为boolean。</p>     <p>如果obj是className类或其子类的实例，则返回值为true；否则，返回值为false。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div </li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Bird</span> <span <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'true'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 7525px;">     <h3 id="语句">语句<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="语句" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>if语句</strong></p>     <p>if语句用于需要根据逻辑条件执行不同语句的场景。当逻辑条件为真时，执行对应的一组语句，否则执行另一组语句（如果有的话）。</p>     <p>else部分也可以包含if语句。</p>     <p>if语句如下所示：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (condition1) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// 语句1</span></li><li>} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (condition2) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// 语句2</span></li><li>} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// else语句</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>条件表达式可以是任何类型，非boolean类型会进行隐式类型转换：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s1 = <span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (s1) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(s1); <span class="hljs-comment">// 打印“Hello”</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s2 = <span class="hljs-string">'World'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (s2.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> != <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(s2); <span class="hljs-comment">// 打印“World”</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>switch语句</strong></p>     <p>使用switch语句执行与switch表达式值匹配的代码块。</p>     <p>switch语句如下所示：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (expression) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-attr">label1</span>: <span class="hljs-comment">// 如果label1匹配，则执行</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 语句1</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 可省略</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-attr">label2</span>:</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-attr">label3</span>: <span class="hljs-comment">// 如果label2或label3匹配，则执行</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 语句23</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 可省略</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">default</span>:</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 默认语句</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果switch表达式的值等于某个label的值，则执行相应的语句。</p>     <p>如果没有任何一个label值与表达式值相匹配，并且switch具有default子句，那么程序会执行default子句对应的代码块。</p>     <p>break语句（可选的）允许跳出switch语句并继续执行switch语句之后的语句。</p>     <p>如果没有break语句，则执行switch中的下一个label对应的代码块。</p>     <p><strong>条件表达式</strong></p>     <p>条件表达式根据第一个表达式的布尔值来返回其他两个表达式之一的结果。</p>     <p>示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>condition ? expression1 : expression2</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果condition的值为真值（转换后为true的值），则使用expression1作为该表达式的结果；否则，使用expression2作为该表达式的结果。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> message = <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">random</span>() &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'Valid'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'Failed'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>condition如果是非bool值则会进行隐式转换。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'true'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'false'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">''</span> ? <span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-number">1</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'true'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'false'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// true</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'true'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'false'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// false</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'true'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'false'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// false</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">'true'</span> : <span class="hljs-string">'false'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// false</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>for语句</strong></p>     <p>for语句会被重复执行，直到循环退出语句值为false。</p>     <p>for语句如下所示：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ([init]; [condition]; [update]) {</li><li>  statements</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>for语句的执行流程如下：</p>     <p>1、 执行init表达式（如有）。此表达式通常初始化一个或多个循环计数器。</p>     <p>2、 计算condition。如果它为真值（转换后为true的值），则执行循环主体的语句。如果它为假值（转换后为false的值），则for循环终止。</p>     <p>3、 执行循环主体的语句。</p>     <p>4、 如果有update表达式，则执行该表达式。</p>     <p>5、 返回步骤2。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> sum = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; i += <span class="hljs-number">2</span>) {</li><li>  sum += i;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>for-of语句</strong></p>     <p>使用for-of语句可遍历数组、Set、Map、字符串等可迭代的类型。示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (forVar <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">IterableExpression</span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// process forVar</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button
