    <h2 id="函数">函数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 488px;">     <h3 id="函数声明" class="firsth2">函数声明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数声明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>函数声明引入一个函数，包含其名称、参数列表、返回类型和函数体。</p>     <p>以下示例是一个简单的函数和它的语法语义说明：</p>     <p>1.参数类型标注：x: string, y: string 显式声明参数类型为字符串类型。</p>     <p>2.返回值类型：: string 指定函数返回值为字符串类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, y: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">z</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">`<span class="hljs-subst">${x}</span> <span class="hljs-subst">${y}</span>`</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> z;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在函数声明中，必须为每个参数标记类型。如果参数为可选参数，那么允许在调用函数时省略该参数。函数的最后一个参数可以是rest参数。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 601px;">     <h3 id="可选参数">可选参数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="可选参数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>可选参数的格式可为name?: Type。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">hello</span>(<span class="hljs-params">name?: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (name == <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello!'</span>);</li><li>  } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Hello, <span class="hljs-subst">${name}</span>!`</span>);</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>可选参数的另一种形式为设置的参数默认值。如果在函数调用中这个参数被省略了，则会使用此参数的默认值作为实参。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">multiply</span>(<span class="hljs-params">n: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, coeff: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">2</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> n * coeff;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">multiply</span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>);  <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回2*2</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">multiply</span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回2*3</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 445px;">     <h3 id="rest参数">rest参数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="rest参数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>函数的最后一个参数可以是rest参数，格式为...restName: Type[]。rest参数允许函数接收一个不定长数组，用于处理不定数量的参数输入。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">sum</span>(<span class="hljs-params">...numbers: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>[]</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> res = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> n <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> numbers) {</li><li>    res += n;</li><li>  }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> res;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">sum</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回0</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">sum</span>(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回6</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 529px;">     <h3 id="返回类型">返回类型<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="返回类型" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>如果可以从函数体内推断出函数返回类型，则可在函数声明中省略标注返回类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 显式指定返回类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'foo'</span>; }</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 推断返回类型为string</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">goo</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'goo'</span>; }</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>不需要返回值的函数的返回类型可以显式指定为void或省略标注。这类函数不需要返回语句。</p>     <p>以下示例中两种函数声明方式都是有效的：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">hi1</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'hi'</span>); }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">hi2</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'hi'</span>); }</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 421px;">     <h3 id="函数的作用域">函数的作用域<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数的作用域" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>函数中定义的变量和其他实例仅可以在函数内部访问，不能从外部访问。</p>     <p>如果函数中定义的变量与外部作用域中已有实例同名，则函数内的局部变量定义将覆盖外部定义。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> outerVar = <span class="hljs-string">'I am outer '</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">func</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> outerVar = <span class="hljs-string">'I am inside'</span>;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(outerVar); <span class="hljs-comment">// 输出: I am inside</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">func</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 505px;">     <h3 id="函数调用">函数调用<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数调用" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>调用函数以执行其函数体，实参值会赋值给函数的形参。</p>     <p>如果函数定义如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">join</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, y: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">z</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">`<span class="hljs-subst">${x}</span> <span class="hljs-subst">${y}</span>`</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> z;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>则此函数的调用需要包含两个string类型的参数：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> x = <span class="hljs-title function_">join</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'world'</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(x); <span class="hljs-comment">// 输出: hello world</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 349px;">     <h3 id="函数类型">函数类型<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数类型" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>函数类型通常用于定义回调函数：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> trigFunc = <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 这是一个函数类型</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">do_action</span>(<span class="hljs-params">f: trigFunc</span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">f</span>(<span class="hljs-number">3.141592653589</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 调用函数</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">do_action</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property">sin</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 将函数作为参数传入</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 481px;">     <h3 id="箭头函数又名lambda函数">箭头函数（又名Lambda函数）<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="箭头函数又名lambda函数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>函数可以定义为箭头函数，例如：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> sum = (<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>): <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-params">number</span> =&gt;</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> x + y;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>箭头函数的返回类型可以省略，此时返回类型从函数体推断。</p>     <p>表达式可以指定为箭头函数，使表达更简短，因此以下两种表达方式是等价的：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">sum1</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, y: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) =&gt; { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> x + y; }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">sum2</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, y: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) =&gt; x + y</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 445px;">     <h3 id="闭包">闭包<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="闭包" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>闭包是由函数及声明该函数的环境组合而成的。该环境包含了这个闭包创建时作用域内的任何局部变量。</p>     <p>在下例中，f函数返回了一个闭包，它捕获了count变量，每次调用z，count的值会被保留并递增。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">f</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>): <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> count = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> g = (): <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-params">number</span> =&gt;</span> { count++; <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> count; };</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> g;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> z = <span class="hljs-title function_">f</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">z</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回：1</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">z</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回：2</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 416px;">     <h3 id="函数重载">函数重载<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="函数重载" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>可以通过编写重载，指定函数的不同调用方式。具体方法是，为同一个函数写入多个同名但签名不同的函数头，函数实现紧随其后。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;            <span class="hljs-comment">/* 第一个函数定义 */</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;            <span class="hljs-comment">/* 第二个函数定义 */</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> | <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 函数实现 */</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-number">123</span>);     <span class="hljs-comment">//  OK，使用第一个定义</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'aa'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，使用第二个定义</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>不允许重载函数有相同的名字和参数列表，否则将导致编译错误。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 949px;">     <h2 id="类">类<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="类" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>类声明引入一个新类型，并定义其字段、方法和构造函数。</p>     <p>在以下示例中，定义了Person类，该类具有字段name和surname、构造函数和方法fullName：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span> (<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-property">name</span> + <span class="hljs-string">' '</span> + <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">surname</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>定义类后，可以使用关键字new创建实例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">p</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span> = {<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>};</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3812px;">     <h3 id="字段" class="firsth2">字段<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="字段" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>字段是直接在类中声明的某种类型的变量。</p>     <p>类可以具有实例字段或者静态字段。</p>     <p><strong>实例字段</strong></p>     <p>实例字段存在于类的每个实例上。每个实例都有自己的实例字段集合。</p>     <p>要访问实例字段，需要使用类的实例。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">age</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">n: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, a: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span> = n;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">age</span> = a;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> p1 = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">25</span>);</li><li>p1.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Alice</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> p2 = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">28</span>);</li><li>p2.<span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Bob</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>静态字段</strong></p>     <p>使用关键字static将字段声明为静态。静态字段属于类本身，类的所有实例共享一个静态字段。</p>     <p>要访问静态字段，需要使用类名：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> numberOfPersons = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>     <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>     <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>.<span class="hljs-property">numberOfPersons</span>++;</li><li>     <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>.<span class="hljs-property">numberOfPersons</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>字段初始化</strong></p>     <p>为了减少运行时错误并提升执行性能，</p>     <p>ArkTS要求所有字段在声明时或构造函数中显式初始化，与标准TS的strictPropertyInitialization模式相同。</p>     <p>以下代码在ArkTS中不合法。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// undefined</span></li><li>  </li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">setName</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span> = n;</li><li>  }</li><li>  </li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 开发者使用"string"作为返回类型，这隐藏了name可能为"undefined"的事实。</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 更合适的做法是将返回类型标注为"string | undefined"，以告诉开发者这个API所有可能的返回值。</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> jack = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 假设代码中没有对name赋值，即没有调用"jack.setName('Jack')"</span></li><li>jack.<span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>().<span class="hljs-property">length</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 运行时异常：name is undefined</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在ArkTS中，开发者应该这样写代码。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  </li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">setName</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span> = n;</li><li>  }</li><li>  </li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// 类型为'string'，不可能为"null"或者"undefined"</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>  </li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> jack = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 假设代码中没有对name赋值，即没有调用"jack.setName('Jack')"</span></li><li>jack.<span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>().<span class="hljs-property">length</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 0, 没有运行时异常</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>接下来的代码示例展示了当name的值可能为undefined时，如何正确编写代码。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  name?: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 可能为`undefined`</span></li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">setName</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span> = n;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误：name可以是"undefined"，所以这个API的返回值类型不能仅定义为string类型</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getNameWrong</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// 返回类型匹配name的类型</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> jack = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 假设代码中没有对name赋值，即没有调用"jack.setName('Jack')"</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误：编译器认为下一行代码有可能会访问undefined的属性，报错</span></li><li>jack.<span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>().<span class="hljs-property">length</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译失败</span></li><li>
</li><li>jack.<span class="hljs-title function_">getName</span>()?.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译成功，没有运行时错误</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>getter和setter</strong></p>     <p>setter和getter可用于提供对类属性的受控访问。</p>     <p>在以下示例中，setter用于禁止将_age属性设置为无效值：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">_age</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">age</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_age</span>; }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">age</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (x &lt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Invalid age argument'</span>);</li><li>    }</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_age</span> = x;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> p = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>();</li><li>p.<span class="hljs-property">age</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 输出0</span></li><li>p.<span class="hljs-property">age</span> = -<span class="hljs-number">42</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 设置无效age值会抛出错误</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在类中可以定义getter或者setter。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 4064px;">     <h3 id="方法">方法<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="方法" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>方法属于类。类可以定义实例方法或者静态方法。静态方法属于类本身，只能访问静态字段。而实例方法既可以访问静态字段，也可以访问实例字段，包括类的私有字段。</p>     <p><strong>实例方法</strong></p>     <p>以下示例说明了实例方法的工作原理。</p>     <p>calculateArea方法计算矩形面积：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RectangleSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">height</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">height: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, width: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">height</span> = height;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">width</span> = width;</li><li>  }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateArea</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">height</span> * <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">width</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>必须通过类的实例调用实例方法：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> square = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RectangleSize</span>(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">10</span>);</li><li>square.<span class="hljs-title function_">calculateArea</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 输出：100</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>静态方法</strong></p>     <p>使用关键字 static 声明静态方法。静态方法属于类，只能访问静态字段。</p>     <p>静态方法定义了类作为一个整体的公共行为。</p>     <p>必须通过类名调用静态方法：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cl</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'this is a static method.'</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Cl</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">staticMethod</span>());</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>继承</strong></p>     <p>一个类可以继承另一个类（称为基类），并使用以下语法实现多个接口：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> [<span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">BaseClassName</span>] [<span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> listOfInterfaces] {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>继承类继承基类的字段和方法，但不继承构造函数。继承类可以新增定义字段和方法，也可以覆盖其基类定义的方法。</p>     <p>基类也称为“父类”或“超类”。继承类也称为“派生类”或“子类”。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> _age = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">age</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_age</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Employee</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_ inherited__">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">salary</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateTaxes</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">salary</span> * <span class="hljs-number">0.42</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>包含implements子句的类必须实现列出的接口中定义的所有方法，但使用默认实现定义的方法除外。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">DateInterface</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">now</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyDate</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">DateInterface</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">now</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 在此实现</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'now'</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>父类访问</strong></p>     <p>关键字super可用于访问父类的方法和构造函数。在实现子类功能时，可以通过该关键字从父类中获取所需接口：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RectangleSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-attr">height</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span> (<span class="hljs-attr">h</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">w</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">height</span> = h;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">width</span> = w;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">/* 绘制边界 */</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">FilledRectangle</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_ inherited__">RectangleSize</span> {</li><li>  color = <span class="hljs-string">''</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span> (<span class="hljs-attr">h</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">w</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">c</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">super</span>(h, w); <span class="hljs-comment">// 父类构造函数的调用</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">color</span> = c;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">super</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">draw</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 父类方法的调用</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">/* 填充矩形 */</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>方法重写</strong></p>     <p>子类可以重写其父类中定义的方法的实现。重写的方法必须具有与原始方法相同的参数类型和相同或派生的返回类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RectangleSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">area</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 实现</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Square</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_ inherited__">RectangleSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">side</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">area</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">side</span> * <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">side</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>方法重载签名</strong></p>     <p>通过重载签名，指定方法的不同调用。具体方法为，为同一个方法写入多个同名但签名不同的方法头，方法实现紧随其后。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;            <span class="hljs-comment">/* 第一个签名 */</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;            <span class="hljs-comment">/* 第二个签名 */</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> | <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 实现签名 */</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> c = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">C</span>();</li><li>c.<span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-number">123</span>);     <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，使用第一个签名</span></li><li>c.<span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'aa'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，使用第二个签名</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果两个重载签名的名称和参数列表均相同，则为错误。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1460px;">     <h3 id="构造函数">构造函数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="构造函数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>类声明可以包含用于初始化对象状态的构造函数。</p>     <p>构造函数定义如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果未定义构造函数，则会自动创建具有空参数列表的默认构造函数，例如：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class_">Point</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在这种情况下，默认构造函数使用字段类型的默认值初始化实例中的字段。</p>     <p><strong>派生类的构造函数</strong></p>     <p>构造函数函数体的第一条语句可以使用关键字super来显式调用直接父类的构造函数。</p>     <div <p><strong>构造函数重载签名</strong></p>     <p>可以通过编写重载签名，指定构造函数的不同调用方式。具体方法是，为同一个构造函数写入多个同名但签名不同的构造函数头，构造函数实现紧随其后。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" function_">C</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'abc'</span>);    <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，使用第二个签名</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果两个重载签名的名称和参数列表均相同，则为错误。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1081px;">     <h3 id="可见性修饰符">可见性修饰符<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="可见性修饰符" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>类的方法和属性都可以使用可见性修饰符。</p>     <p>可见性修饰符包括：private、protected和public。默认可见性为public。</p>     <p><strong>Public（公有）</strong></p>     <p>public修饰的类成员（字段、方法、构造函数）在程序的任何可访问该类的地方都是可见的。</p>     <p><strong>Private（私有）</strong></p>     <p>private修饰的成员不能在声明该成员的类之外访问，例如：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  set_y (<span class="hljs-attr">new_y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> = new_y; <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，因为y在类本身中可以访问</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> c = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">C</span>();</li><li>c.<span class="hljs-property">x</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，该字段是公有的</span></li><li>c.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误：'y'不可见</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>Protected（受保护）</strong></p>     <p>protected修饰符的作用与private修饰符非常相似，不同点是protected修饰的成员允许在派生类中访问，例如：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Base</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// OK，访问受保护成员</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> = <span style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1789px;">     <h3 id="对象字面量">对象字面量<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="对象字面量" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>对象字面量是一个表达式，可用于创建类实例并提供一些初始值。它在某些情况下更方便，可以用来代替new表达式。</p>     <p>对象字面量的表示方式是：封闭在花括号对({})中的'属性名：值'的列表。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">c</span>: C = {<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'foo'</span>};</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>ArkTS是静态类型语言，如上述示例所示，对象字面量只能在可以推导出该字面量类型的上下文中使用。其他正确的例子如下所示：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">c: C</span>) {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">c</span>: C</li><li>
</li><li>c = {<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'foo'</span>};  <span class="hljs-comment">// 使用变量的类型</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'foo'</span>}); <span class="hljs-comment">// 使用参数的类型</span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">bar</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>): C {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> {<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'foo'</span>}; <span class="hljs-comment">// 使用返回类型</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>也可以在数组元素类型或类字段类型中使用：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>}, {<span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">s</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>}];</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>Record类型的对象字面量</strong></p>     <p>泛型Record&lt;K, V&gt;用于将类型（键类型）的属性映射到另一个类型（值类型）。常用对象字面量来初始化该类型的值：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">map</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'John'</span>: <span </li><li>map[<span class="hljs-string">'John'</span>]; <span class="hljs-comment">// 25</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>类型K可以是字符串类型或数值类型(不包括BigInt)，而V可以是任何类型。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">PersonInfo</span> {</li><li>  <span
