class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">map</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">PersonInfo</span>&gt; = {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'John'</span>: { <span class="hljs-attr">age</span>: <span class="hljs-number">25</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">salary</span>: <span class="hljs-number">10</span>},</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'Mary'</span>: { <span class="hljs-attr">age</span>: <span class="hljs-number">21</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">salary</span>: <span class="hljs-number">20</span>}</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1213px;">     <h3 id="抽象类">抽象类<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="抽象类" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>带有abstract修饰符的类称为抽象类。抽象类可用于表示一组更具体的概念所共有的概念。</p>     <p>尝试创建抽象类的实例会导致编译错误：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">X</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">field</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">p: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">field</span> = p;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> x = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">X</span>(<span class="hljs-number">666</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment">//编译时错误：不能创建抽象类的具体实例</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>抽象类的子类可以是抽象类也可以是非抽象类。抽象父类的非抽象子类可以实例化。因此，执行抽象类的构造函数和该类非静态字段的字段初始化器：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Base</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">field</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">p: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">field</span> = p;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Derived</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_ inherited__">Base</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">p: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">super</span>(p);</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> x = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Derived</span>(<span class="hljs-number">666</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>抽象方法</strong></p>     <p>带有abstract修饰符的方法称为抽象方法，抽象方法可以被声明但不能被实现。</p>     <p>只有抽象类内才能有抽象方法，如果非抽象类具有抽象方法，则会发生编译时错误：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Y</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">method</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">p</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment">//编译时错误：抽象方法只能在抽象类内。</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1081px;">     <h2 id="接口">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>接口声明引入新类型。接口是定义代码协定的常见方式。</p>     <p>任何类的实例，只要实现了特定接口，即可通过该接口实现多态。</p>     <p>接口通常包含属性和方法的声明。</p>     <p>示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 属性</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">AreaSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateAreaSize</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 方法的声明</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">someMethod</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;     <span class="hljs-comment">// 方法的声明</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>实现接口的类示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 接口：</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">AreaSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateAreaSize</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 方法的声明</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">someMethod</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;     <span class="hljs-comment">// 方法的声明</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 实现：</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RectangleSize</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">AreaSize</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">height</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">someMethod</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'someMethod called'</span>);</li><li>  }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateAreaSize</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">someMethod</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// 调用另一个方法并返回结果</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">width</span> * <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">height</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1081px;">     <h3 id="接口属性" class="firsth2">接口属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>接口属性可以是字段、getter、setter或getter和setter组合的形式。</p>     <p>属性字段只是getter/setter对的便捷写法。以下表达方式是等价的：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">color</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">color</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>);</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>实现接口的类也可以使用以下两种方式：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">StyledRectangle</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">StyledRectangle</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">_color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">color</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_color</span>; }</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">color</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>) { <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_color</span> = x; }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 392px;">     <h3 id="接口继承">接口继承<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口继承" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>接口可以继承其他接口，示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ExtendedStyle</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Style</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>继承接口包含被继承接口的所有属性和方法，还可以添加自己的属性和方法。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1441px;">     <h3 id="抽象类和接口">抽象类和接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="抽象类和接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>抽象类与接口都无法实例化。抽象类是类的抽象，抽象类用来捕捉子类的通用特性，接口是行为的抽象。在ArkTS语法中抽象类与接口的区别如下：</p>     <ul>      <li>一个类只能继承一个抽象类，而一个类可以实现一个或多个接口；</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// Bird类继承Animal抽象类并实现多个接口CanFly、CanSwim</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Bird</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_ inherited__">Animal</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CanFly</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">CanSwim</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>接口中不能含有静态代码块以及静态方法，而抽象类可以有静态代码块和静态方法；</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyInterface</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 错误：接口中不能包含静态成员</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">staticMethod</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 错误：接口中不能包含静态代码块</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'static'</span>); };</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAbstractClass</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 正确：抽象类可以有静态方法</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">staticMethod</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'static'</span>); }</li><li>
</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// 正确：抽象类可以有静态代码块</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'static initialization block'</span>); }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>抽象类里面可以有方法的实现，但是接口没有方法的实现，是完全抽象的；</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAbstractClass</span> {</li><li>   <span class="hljs-comment">// 正确：抽象类里面可以有方法的实现</span></li><li>   <span class="hljs-title function_">func</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'func'</span>); }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyInterface</span> {</li><li>   <span class="hljs-comment">// 错误：接口没有方法的实现，是完全抽象的</span></li><li>   <span class="hljs-title function_">func</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'func'</span>); }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>抽象类可以有构造函数，而接口不能有构造函数。</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAbstractClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>){}  <span class="hljs-comment">// 正确：抽象类可以有构造函数</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyInterface</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 错误：接口中不能有构造函数</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 116px;">     <h2 id="泛型类型和函数">泛型类型和函数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="泛型类型和函数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>泛型类型和函数使代码能够以类型安全的方式操作多种数据类型，而无需为每种类型编写重复的逻辑。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="泛型类和接口" class="firsth2">泛型类和接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="泛型类和接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>类和接口可以定义为泛型，将参数添加到类型定义中。如以下示例中的类型参数Element：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CustomStack</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Element</span>&gt; {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">e</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Element</span>):<span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>要使用类型CustomStack，必须为每个类型参数指定类型实参：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CustomStack</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>&gt;();</li><li>s.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>编译器在使用泛型类型和函数时会确保类型安全。参见以下示例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> s = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CustomStack</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>&gt;();</li><li>s.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>(<span class="hljs-number">55</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 将会产生编译时错误</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 464px;">     <h3 id="泛型约束">泛型约束<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="泛型约束" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>泛型类型的类型参数可以被限制只能取某些特定的值。例如，MyHashMap&lt;Key, Value&gt;这个类中的Key类型参数必须具有hash方法。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Hashable</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">hash</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyHashMap</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-title function_">hash</span>();</li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...其他代码...</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在上面的例子中，Key类型扩展了Hashable，Hashable接口的所有方法都可以为key调用。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 829px;">     <h3 id="泛型函数">泛型函数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="泛型函数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>使用泛型函数可编写更通用的代码。比如返回数组最后一个元素的函数：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">last</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>];</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">last</span>([<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>]); <span class="hljs-comment">// 3</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果需要为任何数组定义相同的函数，使用类型参数将该函数定义为泛型：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> last&lt;T&gt;(<span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: T[]): T {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> x[x.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>];</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>现在，该函数可以与任何数组一起使用。</p>     <p>在函数调用中，类型实参可以显式或隐式设置：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 显式设置的类型实参</span></li><li><span last&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt;([<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>]);</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 隐式设置的类型实参</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 编译器根据调用参数的类型来确定类型实参</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-number">3</span>]);</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="泛型默认值">泛型默认值<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="泛型默认值" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>泛型类型的类型参数可以设置默认值，这样无需指定实际类型实参，直接使用泛型类型名称即可。以下示例展示了类和函数的这一特性。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">SomeType</span> {}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Interface</span> &lt;T1 = <span class="hljs-title class_">SomeType</span>&gt; { }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Base</span> &lt;<span class="hljs-variable constant_">T2</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">SomeType</span>&gt; { }</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Interface</span> { }</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// Derived1在语义上等价于Derived2</span></li><li><span }</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> foo&lt;T = <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt;(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>();</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 此函数在语义上等价于下面的调用</span></li><li>foo&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt;();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 553px;">     <h2 id="空安全">空安全<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="空安全" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>默认情况下，ArkTS中的所有类型都不允许为空，这类似于TypeScript的(strictNullChecks)模式，但规则更严格。</p>     <p>在下面的示例中，所有行都会导致编译时错误：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;    <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;    <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">z</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>[] = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>可以为空值的变量定义为联合类型T | null。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;</li><li>x = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;    <span class="hljs-comment">// ok</span></li><li>x = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// ok</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (x != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) { <span class="hljs-comment">/* do something */</span> }</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 421px;">     <h3 id="非空断言运算符" class="firsth2">非空断言运算符<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="非空断言运算符" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>后缀运算符!可用于断言其操作数为非空。</p>     <p>当应用于可空类型的值时，编译时类型会变为非空类型。例如，类型从T | null变为T：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">A</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">a: A | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span></span>) {</li><li>  a.<span class="hljs-property">value</span>;   <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误：无法访问可空值的属性</span></li><li>  a!.<span class="hljs-property">value</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译通过，如果运行时a的值非空，可以访问到a的属性；如果运行时a的值为空，则发生运行时异常</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 469px;">     <h3 id="空值合并运算符">空值合并运算符<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="空值合并运算符" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>空值合并二元运算符??用于检查左侧表达式的求值是否等于null或者undefined。如果是，则表达式的结果为右侧表达式；否则，结果为左侧表达式。</p>     <p>换句话说，a ?? b等价于三元运算符(a != null &amp;&amp; a != undefined) ? a : b。</p>     <p>在以下示例中，getNick方法返回已设置的昵称。如果未设置，则返回空字符串。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">nick</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getNick</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">nick</span> ?? <span class="hljs-string">''</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1129px;">     <h3 id="可选链">可选链<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="可选链" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>访问对象属性时，如果属性是undefined或null，可选链运算符返回undefined。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">nick</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;</li><li>  spouse?: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span></li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">setSpouse</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">spouse</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">spouse</span> = spouse;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getSpouseNick</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">spouse</span>?.<span class="hljs-property">nick</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">nick: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">nick</span> = nick;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">spouse</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>说明</strong>：getSpouseNick的返回类型必须为string | null | undefined，因为该方法在某些情况下会返回null或undefined。</p>     <p>可选链可以任意长，可以包含任意数量的?.运算符。</p>     <p>在以下示例中，如果Person实例的spouse属性不为空，并且spouse的nick属性也不为空时，输出spouse.nick。否则，输出undefined。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> {</li><li>  <span class_">Person</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">nick: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">nick</span> = nick;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">spouse</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">p</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Person</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title undefined</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 212px;">     <h2 id="模块">模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>程序可划分为多组编译单元或模块。</p>     <p>每个模块都有其自己的作用域，即在模块中创建的任何声明（变量、函数、类等）在该模块之外都不可见，除非它们被显式导出。</p>     <p>与此相对，必须首先将另一个模块导出的变量、函数、类、接口等导入到当前模块中。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 769px;">     <h3 id="导出" class="firsth2">导出<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导出" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>可以使用关键字export导出顶层的声明。</p>     <p>未导出的声明名称被视为私有名称，只能在声明该名称的模块中使用。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">x</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">y</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">constructor</span>(<span class="hljs-params">x: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, y: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">x</span> = x;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> = y;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Origin</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Point</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Distance</span>(<span class="hljs-params">p1: Point, p2: Point</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sqrt</span>((p2.<span class="hljs-property">x</span> - p1.<span class="hljs-property">x</span>) * (p2.<span class="hljs-property">x</span> - p1.<span class="hljs-property">x</span>) + (p2.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> - p1.<span class="hljs-property">y</span>) * (p2.<span class="hljs-property">y</span> - p1.<span class="hljs-property">y</span>));</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>导出默认导出的对象</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Demo</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2236px;">     <h3 id="导入">导入<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>静态导入</strong></p>     <p>导入声明用于导入从其他模块导出的实体，并在当前模块中提供其绑定。导入声明由两部分组成：</p>     <ul>      <li>导入路径，用于指定导入的模块；</li>      <li>导入绑定，用于定义导入的模块中的可用实体集和使用形式（限定或不限定使用）。</li>     </ul>     <p>导入绑定可以有几种形式。</p>     <p>假设模块的路径为“./utils”，并且导出了实体“X”和“Y”。</p>     <p>导入绑定* as A表示绑定名称“A”，通过A.name可访问从导入路径指定的模块导出的所有实体：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> * <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Utils</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./utils'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-title class_">Utils</span>.<span class="hljs-property">X</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自Utils的X</span></li><li><span class="hljs-title class_">Utils</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Y</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自Utils的Y</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>导入绑定{ ident1, ..., identN }表示将导出的实体与指定名称绑定，该名称可以用作简单名称：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { X, Y } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./utils'</span>;</li><li>X <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自utils的X</span></li><li>Y <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自utils的Y</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果标识符列表定义了ident as alias，则实体ident将绑定在名称alias下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { X <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> Z, Y } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./utils'</span>;</li><li>Z <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自Utils的X</span></li><li>Y <span class="hljs-comment">// 表示来自Utils的Y</span></li><li>X <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误：'X'不可见</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>动态导入</strong></p>     <p>在应用开发的有些场景中，如果希望根据条件导入模块或者按需导入模块，可以使用动态导入代替静态导入。</p>     <p>import()语法被称为动态导入（dynamic import），是一种类似函数的表达式，用于动态导入模块。调用这种方式，会返回一个promise。</p>     <p>如下例所示，import(modulePath)可以加载模块并返回一个promise，该promise resolve为一个包含其所有导出的模块对象。该表达式可以在代码中的任意位置调用。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// Calc.ts</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span>(<span class="hljs-params">a:<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, b:<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>):<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> c = a + b;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Dynamic import, %d + %d = %d'</span>, a, b, c);</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> c;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// Index.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'./Calc'</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">then</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">obj: ESObject</span>) =&gt;</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(obj.<span class="hljs-title function_">add</span>(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>));</li><li>}).<span class="hljs-title function_">catch</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">err: <span class="hljs-built_in">Error</span></span>) =&gt;</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Module dynamic import error: '</span>, err);</li><li>});</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果在异步函数中，可以使用let module = await import(modulePath)。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// say.ts</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">bye</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Bye'</span>);</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>那么，可以像下面这样进行动态导入：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">async</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> ns = <span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'./say'</span>);</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> hi = ns.<span class="hljs-property">hi</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> bye = ns.<span
