<p>更多的使用动态import的业务场景和使用实例见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-dynamic-import">动态import</a>。</p>    </div>    <p><strong>导入HarmonyOS SDK的开放能力</strong></p>    <p>HarmonyOS SDK提供的开放能力（接口）也需要在导入声明后使用。可直接导入接口模块来使用该模块内的所有接口能力，例如：</p>    <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="ts" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">UIAbility</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@ohos.app.ability.UIAbility'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    <p>从HarmonyOS NEXT Developer Preview 1版本开始引入Kit概念。SDK对同一个Kit下的接口模块进行了封装，开发者在示例代码中可通过导入Kit的方式来使用Kit所包含的接口能力。其中，Kit封装的接口模块可查看SDK目录下Kit子目录中各Kit的定义。在代码开发中，推荐通过导入Kit方式使用开放能力。</p>    <p>通过导入Kit方式使用开放能力有三种方式：</p>    <ul>     <li>      <p>方式一：导入Kit下单个模块的接口能力。例如：</p>      <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="ts" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">UIAbility</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.AbilityKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>     <li>      <p>方式二：导入Kit下多个模块的接口能力。例如：</p>      <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="ts" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">UIAbility</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Ability</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Context</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.AbilityKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>     <li>      <p>方式三：导入Kit包含的所有模块的接口能力。例如：</p>      <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="ts" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> * <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">module</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.AbilityKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>      <p>其中，“module”为别名，可自定义，然后通过该名称调用模块的接口。</p>      <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">        <p>方式三可能会导入过多无需使用的模块，导致编译后的HAP包太大，占用过多资源，请谨慎使用。</p>       </div></div></div></li>    </ul>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 92px;">     <h3 id="顶层语句">顶层语句<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="顶层语句" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>顶层语句是指在模块最外层编写的语句，不被任何函数、类或块级作用域包裹。这些语句包括变量声明、函数声明和表达式。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 80px;">     <h2 id="关键字">关键字<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="关键字" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1020px;">     <h3 id="this" class="firsth2">this<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="this" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>关键字this只能在类的实例方法中使用。</p>     <p><strong>示例</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">A</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">count</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">m</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">i</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">count</span> = i;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>使用限制：</p>     <ul>      <li>不支持this类型</li>      <li>不支持在函数和类的静态方法中使用this</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>示例</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">A</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">n</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">f1</span>(<span class="hljs-params">arg1: <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span></span>) {} <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误，不支持this类型</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">f2</span>(<span class="hljs-params">arg1: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">n</span> = arg1;  <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误，不支持在类的静态方法中使用this</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">arg1: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">n</span> = i;       <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译时错误，不支持在函数中使用this</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>关键字this的指向:</p>     <ul>      <li>调用实例方法的对象</li>      <li>正在构造的对象</li>     </ul>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1420px;">     <h2 id="注解">注解<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="注解" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>注解（Annotation）是一种语言特性，它通过添加元数据来改变应用声明的语义。</p>     <p>注解的声明和使用如下所示：</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 注解的声明：</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 注解的使用：</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>使用@interface声明注解。</li>      <li>注解ClassAuthor需要将元信息添加到类声明中。</li>      <li>注解必须放置在声明之前。</li>      <li>注解可以包含上述示例中所示的参数。</li>     </ul>     <p>对于要使用的注解，其名称必须以符号@（例如：@MyAnno）为前缀。符号@和名称之间不允许有空格和行分隔符。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解需要'@'为前缀</span></li><li>@ <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：符号`@`和名称之间不允许有空格和行分隔符</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果在使用位置无法访问注解名称，则会发生编译错误。</p>     <p>注解声明可以导出并在其他文件中使用。</p>     <p>多个注解可以应用于同一个声明（注解间的先后顺序不影响使用）。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>()</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"John Smith"</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>注解不是Typescript中的特性，只能在.ets/.d.ets文件中使用。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>应用开发中，在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-hvigor-build-har#section19788284410" target="_blank">release模式下构建</a>源码HAR，并同时<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/source-obfuscation">开启混淆</a>时，由于编译产物为JS文件，而在JS中没有注解的实现机制，因此会在编译过程中被移除，导致无法通过注解实现AOP插桩。</p>       <p>为避免因此引起的功能异常，禁止在JS HAR(编译产物中存在JS的HAR包)中使用注解。</p>       <p>如果需要在release模式并且开启混淆的情况下构建含有注解的HAR包，可以构建<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-hvigor-build-har#section16598338112415" target="_blank">字节码HAR</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 10305px;">     <h3 id="用户自定义注解" class="firsth2">用户自定义注解<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="用户自定义注解" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>从API version 20及之后版本，支持用户自定义注解。</strong></p>     <p><strong>用户自定义注解的声明</strong></p>     <p>用户自定义注解的定义与interface的定义类似，其中的interface关键字以符号@为前缀。</p>     <p>注解字段仅限于下面列举的类型：</p>     <ul>      <li>number</li>      <li>boolean</li>      <li>string</li>      <li>枚举</li>      <li>以上类型的数组       <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">         <ul>          <li>如果使用其他类型用作注解字段的类型，则会发生编译错误。</li>          <li>注解字段类型不支持BigInt。</li>         </ul>        </div></div></div></li>     </ul>     <p>注解字段的默认值必须使用常量表达式来指定。</p>     <p>常量表达式的场景如下所示：</p>     <ul>      <li>数字字面量</li>      <li>布尔字面量</li>      <li>字符串字面量</li>      <li>枚举值（需要在编译时确定值）</li>      <li>以上常量组成的数组       <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">         <p>如果枚举值不能在编译时确定，会编译报错。</p>        </div></div></div></li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ts</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> X {</li><li>  x = <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// x不是编译时能确定的常量</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> {X} <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Position</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = X.<span class="hljs-property">x</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解字段的默认值必须使用常量表达式</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>注解必须定义在顶层作用域（top-level），否则会出现编译报错。</p>     <p>注解的名称不能与注解定义所在作用域内可见的其他实体名称相同，否则会出现编译报错。</p>     <p>注解不支持类型Typescript中的合并，否则会出现编译报错。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> ns {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MataInfo</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解必须定义在顶层作用域</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>  }</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Position</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Position</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解的名称不能与注解定义所在作用域内可见的其他实体名称相同</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解的名称不能与注解定义所在作用域内可见的其他实体名称相同</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>注解不是类型，把注解当类型使用时会出现编译报错（例如：对注解使用类型别名）。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Position</span> {}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Pos</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">Position</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解不是类型</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>注解不支持在类的getter和setter方法中添加，若添加注解会编译报错。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'John Smith'</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-attr">_name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'John Smith'</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解不支持在类的getter和setter方法添加</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">get</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">name</span>() {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_name</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'John Smith'</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解不支持在类的getter和setter方法添加</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">name</span>(<span class="hljs-params">authorName: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">_name</span> = authorName;</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>用户自定义注解的使用</strong></p>     <p>注解声明示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassPreamble</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">revision</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;</li><li>}</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> {}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>当前仅允许对class declarations和method declarations使用注解，对类和方法可以同时使用同一个注解。</p>     <p>注解用法示例如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"John"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">revision</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C1</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// revision的默认值为1</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C2</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>() <span class="hljs-comment">// 对类和方法可以同时使用同一个注解</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C3</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>()</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {}</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>()</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">bar</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {}</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>注解中的字段顺序不影响使用。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"John"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">revision</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// the same as:</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">revision</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"John"</span>})</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>使用注解时，必须给所有没有默认值的字段赋值，否则会发生编译错误。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>赋值应当与注解声明的类型一致，所赋的值与注解字段默认值的要求一样，只能使用常量表达式。</p>      </div></div></div>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>() <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：authorName字段未定义</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C1</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果注解中定义了数组类型的字段，则使用数组字面量来设置该字段的值。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassPreamble</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">revision</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">reviewers</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>[];</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassPreamble</span>(</li><li>  {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-attr">authorName</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Alice"</span>,</li><li>    <span class="hljs-attr">reviewers</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Clara"</span>]</li><li>  }</li><li>)</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C3</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>如果不需要定义注解字段，可以省略注解名称后的括号。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C4</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>导入和导出注解</strong></p>     <p>注解也可以被导入导出。针对导出，当前仅支持在定义时的导出，即export @interface的形式。</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> {}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>针对导入，当前仅支持import {}和import * as两种方式。</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> {}</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> * <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> ns <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ns</span>.<span class="hljs-property">ClassAuthor</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>不允许在import中对注解进行重命名。</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Anno</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：不允许在import中对注解进行重命名</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>不允许对注解使用任何其他形式的 import/export，这会导致编译报错。</p>     <ul>      <li>由于注解不是类型，因此禁止使用type符号进行导入和导出。</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">type</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：注解不允许使用'type'符号进行导入和导出</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <ul>      <li>如果仅从模块导入注解，则不会触发模块的副作用。</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Anno</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>);</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">Anno</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> * <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> ns <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 仅引用了Anno注解，不会导致a.ets的console.info执行</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">X</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>.d.ets文件中的注解</strong></p>     <p>注解可以出现在.d.ets文件中。</p>     <p>可以在.d.ets文件中用环境声明（ambient declaration）来声明注解。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-attr">ambientAnnotationDeclaration</span>:</li><li>  <span class="hljs-string">'declare'</span> userDefinedAnnotationDeclaration</li><li>  ;</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.d.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>上述声明中：</p>     <ul>      <li>不会引入新的注解定义，而是提供注解的类型信息。</li>      <li>注解需定义在其他源代码文件中。</li>      <li>注解的环境声明和实现需要完全一致，包括字段的类型和默认值。</li>     </ul>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.d.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">NameAnno</span>{<span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">""</span>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">NameAnno</span>{<span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">""</span>} <span class="hljs-comment">// ok</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>环境声明的注解和class类似，也可以被import使用。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.d.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MyAnno</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./a'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>编译器自动生成的.d.ets文件</strong></p>     <p>当编译器根据ets代码自动生成.d.ets文件时，存在以下2种情况。</p>     <ol>      <li>当注解定义被导出时，源代码中的注解定义会在.d.ets文件中保留。       <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MethodAnno</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// 没导出</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.d.ets 编译器生成的声明文件</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>      <li>       <p>当下面所有条件成立时，源代码中实体的注解实例会在.d.ets文件中保留。</p>       <p>2.1 注解的定义被导出（import的注解也算作被导出）。</p>       <p>2.2 如果实体是类，则类被导出。</p>       <p>2.3 如果实体是方法，则类被导出，并且方法不是私有方法。</p>       <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'./author'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MethodAnno</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MethodAnno</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-number">123</span>})</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {}</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MethodAnno</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-number">456</span>})</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">bar</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {}</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// a.d.ets 编译器生成的声明文件</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> {<span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span>} <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">"./author"</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MethodAnno</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span> = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;</li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">declare</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MethodAnno</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: <span class="hljs-number">123</span>})</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>  bar; <span class="hljs-comment">// 私有方法不保留注解</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>       <p></p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>开发者生成的.d.ets文件</strong></p>     <p>开发者生成的.d.ets文件中的注解信息不会自动应用到实现的源代码中。</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.d.ets 开发者生成的声明文件</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@ClassAuthor</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 声明文件中有注解</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// b.ets 开发者对声明文件实现的源代码</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@interface</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ClassAuthor</span> {}</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 实现文件中没有注解</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>在最终编译产物中，class C没有注解。</p>     <p><strong>重复注解和继承</strong></p>     <p>同一个实体不能重复使用同一注解，否则会导致编译错误。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"123"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>: <span class="hljs-number">456</span>})</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"321"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>: <span class="hljs-number">654</span>}) <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：不允许重复注释</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>子类不会继承基类的注解，也不会继承基类方法的注解。</p>     <p><strong>注解和抽象类、抽象方法</strong></p>     <p>不支持对抽象类或抽象方法使用注解，否则将导致编译错误。</p>     <div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lxd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" hw-language="typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：不允许在抽象类和抽象方法上使用注解</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">C</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@MyAnno</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(): <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 编译错误：不允许在抽象类和抽象方法上使用注解</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 140px;">     <h2 id="arkui支持">ArkUI支持<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="arkui支持" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>本节演示ArkTS为创建图形用户界面（GUI）程序提供的机制。ArkUI基于TypeScript提供了一系列扩展能力，以声明式地描述应用程序的GUI以及GUI组件间的交互。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 140px;">     <h3 id="arkui示例" class="firsth2">ArkUI示例<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="arkui示例" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-mvvm#代码示例">MVVM代码示例</a>提供了一个完整的基于ArkUI的应用程序，以展示其GUI编程功能。</p>     <p>有关ArkUI功能的更多详细信息，请参见ArkUI<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-basic-syntax-overview">基本语法概述</a>。</p>    </div>   </div>   <div></div></div>
